       <article class="post-4228 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-chicken category-chinese category-featured category-noodles-pasta category-slow-cooker-meals tag-chicken-lo-mien tag-crockpot-meals tag-noodles tag-slow-cooker entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
          Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles
         </h1>
         <p class="entry-meta">
          <time class="entry-time" datetime="2013-12-05T09:26:00+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
           December 5, 2013
          </time>
         </p>
        </header>
        <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
         <div class="pin-it-btn-wrapper">
          <a data-pin-color="red" data-pin-config="none" data-pin-do="buttonBookmark" href="//www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http%3A%2F%2Flifemadesweeter.com%2F2013%2F12%2Feasy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles%2F&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2Flh5.ggpht.com%2F-rllNZqWV2rs%2FUo1apcHy71I%2FAAAAAAAAMPc%2Fi5WNuNUtxXs%2Fs144-o%2FIMG_9701.jpg&amp;description=Best%20easy%20crock-pot%20Chicken%20Lo%20Mein%20Noodles%20is%20easier%2C%20healthier%20%26%20way%20better%20than%20take-out%21%20Our%20favorite%20dish%20all%20made%20in%20the%20the%20slow%20cooker.%20Delicious%21" rel="nobox">
           <img data-pib-button="true" src="//assets.pinterest.com/images/pidgets/pin_it_button.png" title="Pin It"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="shareaholic-canvas" data-app="share_buttons" data-app-id="17598345" data-link="http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/" data-summary="" data-title="Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles">
         </div>
         <p>
          <em>
           The best easiest
           <span style="color: #3366ff;">
            <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/?p=4228" style="color: #3366ff;" target="_blank" title="Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles">
             Chicken Lo Mein
            </a>
           </span>
           ever. Only 15 minutes to prep. No need to order take=out, this is so much quicker, tastier &amp; healthier! Plus its made all in the slow cooker / crockpot.
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span style="color: #ff0000;">
           *** Pictures and recipe were updated October 2014
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh6.ggpht.com/-jIOrJyKq1pk/VDZ6bic9usI/AAAAAAAARiI/pIuCoTDFB3s/s0/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520-%252520by%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog6#6068172161451670210" rel="post-4228">
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
           <img alt="Slow Cooker Chicken Lo Mein {Crockpot} - by @LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh6.ggpht.com/-jIOrJyKq1pk/VDZ6bic9usI/AAAAAAAARiI/pIuCoTDFB3s/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520-%252520by%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh6.ggpht.com/-jIOrJyKq1pk/VDZ6bic9usI/AAAAAAAARiI/pIuCoTDFB3s/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520-%252520by%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </a>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Whats your favorite dish that comes to mind when you think about comfort food?
         </p>
         <p>
          Ours is definitely anything with noodles or pasta. We eat a large
          <strong>
           <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/category/recipes/mains/noodles-pasta/" target="_blank" title="Vietnamese Pho  Beef Rice Noodle Soup (Pho Tai Bo) with Slow Cooker option">
            <span style="color: #3366ff;">
             variety of noodles
            </span>
           </a>
          </strong>
          <span style="color: #3366ff;">
           i
          </span>
          n our house.
         </p>
         <p>
          Its one of my favorite dishes to clean out the fridge with all of those lingering leftovers that you cancustomize by tossing in your favorite veggies or protein.
         </p>
         <p>
          Noodles also make a quick and easy meal which is definitely appreciated during those busy weeknights  its especially perfect for this busy time of year when we are preparing for the holidays.
         </p>
         <p>
          Somehow after a long day of running errands with my kiddos, I didnt feel like standing in front of the stove so I managed to make this
          <strong>
           <span style="color: #3366ff;">
            <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/?p=4228" style="color: #3366ff;" target="_blank" title="Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles">
             Chicken Lo Mein
            </a>
           </span>
          </strong>
          even easier by tossing everything into my slow cooker.
         </p>
         <p>
          Best. Decision.
          <em>
           Ever
          </em>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh4.ggpht.com/-jSoipSGMFhc/VDW27MjCPrI/AAAAAAAARfw/SC1glpmkAmc/s0/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520by%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog6#6067957201048321714" rel="post-4228">
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
           <img alt="Slow Cooker Chicken Lo Mein {Crockpot} by @LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh4.ggpht.com/-jSoipSGMFhc/VDW27MjCPrI/AAAAAAAARfw/SC1glpmkAmc/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520by%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh4.ggpht.com/-jSoipSGMFhc/VDW27MjCPrI/AAAAAAAARfw/SC1glpmkAmc/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520by%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </a>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Simply wash and chop the vegetables and combine it with the sauce and cook on high for about 1 hour or low for about 2 hours.
         </p>
         <p>
          You can even cookthe chicken beforehand but that is completely optional too.
         </p>
         <p>
          I have made them both ways withgreat results but pan frying the chicken on the stove beforehand does give it an additional depth to the flavor. Just make sure you cook the chicken about
          <span style="color: #ff0000;">
           <strong>
            30 minutes
           </strong>
          </span>
          <strong>
           <em>
            prior
           </em>
          </strong>
          to serving the noodles then add it into the slow cooker.
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-Sbr0iF3EO3c/VDW27L1FesI/AAAAAAAARgI/6byLDvH4jM8/s0/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520from%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog6#6067957200855595714" rel="post-4228">
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
           <img alt="Slow Cooker Chicken Lo Mein {Crockpot} from @LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-Sbr0iF3EO3c/VDW27L1FesI/AAAAAAAARgI/6byLDvH4jM8/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520from%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh3.ggpht.com/-Sbr0iF3EO3c/VDW27L1FesI/AAAAAAAARgI/6byLDvH4jM8/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520from%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </a>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Some other tips to note:
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           If you are using
           <span style="color: #0000ff;">
            <strong>
             dry pasta noodles
            </strong>
           </span>
           , you can either cook them first according to the package directions, drain and add them to the slow cooker
           <strong>
            10 minutes
           </strong>
           prior to serving the dish
          </li>
          <li>
           If you are using
           <span style="color: #0000ff;">
            <strong>
             fresh pre-cooked noodles
            </strong>
           </span>
           (I used pre-cooked fresh Lo-Mein noodles), you simply throw the noodles into the slow cooker and turn your slow cooker on high with the rest of the ingredients and sauce for about 10 minutes so the flavors can meld together. Make sure you add the
           <span style="color: #0000ff;">
            <strong>
             fresh pre-cooked
            </strong>
           </span>
           or cooked dry noodles
           <strong>
            NEAR
           </strong>
           the end or
           <strong>
            JUST PRIOR
           </strong>
           to serving will ensure that the noodles will
           <strong>
            NOT
           </strong>
           get too
           <strong>
            <em>
             soft
            </em>
           </strong>
           and
           <strong>
            <em>
             mushy
            </em>
           </strong>
           .
          </li>
         </ul>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Feel free to make it your own with your favorite vegetables. I used
           <span style="color: #008000;">
            <strong>
             baby bok choy
            </strong>
           </span>
           and
           <span style="color: #ff6600;">
            <strong>
             carrots
            </strong>
           </span>
           here and I have also used snow peas, baby corn or bell pepperssuccessfully in the past.
          </li>
         </ul>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Use pork instead of chicken or extra firm or deep fried tofu for a meatless meal. You can find the
           <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/?p=7191" target="_blank" title="{Slow Cooker} Vegetable Lo Mein Noodles + Crock-Pot Slow Cooker Giveaway!">
            <span style="color: #339966;">
             <strong>
              vegetarian version
             </strong>
            </span>
           </a>
           with extra firm tofu
           <span style="color: #339966;">
            <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/?p=7191" style="color: #339966;" target="_blank" title="{Slow Cooker} Vegetable Lo Mein Noodles + Crock-Pot Slow Cooker Giveaway!">
             <strong>
              here.
             </strong>
            </a>
           </span>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
         </p>
         <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh5.ggpht.com/-8nd35ltvxt8/VDW4s7YUb5I/AAAAAAAARh0/0sgNoWw95Fw/s0/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520--%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog6#6067959154945060754" rel="post-4228">
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
           <img alt="Slow Cooker Chicken Lo Mein {Crockpot} -- @LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/-8nd35ltvxt8/VDW4s7YUb5I/AAAAAAAARh0/0sgNoWw95Fw/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520--%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh5.ggpht.com/-8nd35ltvxt8/VDW4s7YUb5I/AAAAAAAARh0/0sgNoWw95Fw/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520--%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </a>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          The flavors are unbelievable and way better and healthier than anything you can buy at a take-out restaurant.
         </p>
         <p>
          You wont believe that this was made in the slow cooker, its the best ever and is by far the MOST popular recipe on this blog.
         </p>
         <p>
          Its been pinned over
          <span style="color: #ff0000;">
           <strong>
            300,000
           </strong>
          </span>
          times so you have got to try making this!
         </p>
         <p>
          This dish makes multiple appearances at our dinner table and I have used several different noodle and vegetable variations.
         </p>
         <p>
          You guys will love how easy dinner is served without having to order Chinese takeout! If you dont have a slow cooker, try my
          <span style="color: #3366ff;">
           <strong>
            <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/2014/01/shrimp-stir-fry-lo-mein-noodles/" style="color: #3366ff;" target="_blank">
             Easy Shrimp Lo Mein noodles
            </a>
           </strong>
          </span>
          that is cooked on the stove top. Just substitute the shrimp with chicken instead.
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p class="clear">
          <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh4.ggpht.com/--AOEirBc3ks/VDW4stgkPAI/AAAAAAAARhw/nXjRSaWVzrM/s0/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520-%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog6#6067959151221554178" rel="post-4228">
           <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
            <img alt="Slow Cooker Chicken Lo Mein {Crockpot} - @LifeMadeSweeter.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh4.ggpht.com/--AOEirBc3ks/VDW4stgkPAI/AAAAAAAARhw/nXjRSaWVzrM/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520-%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg"/>
            <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh4.ggpht.com/--AOEirBc3ks/VDW4stgkPAI/AAAAAAAARhw/nXjRSaWVzrM/w550-o/Slow%252520Cooker%252520Chicken%252520Lo%252520Mein%252520%25257BCrockpot%25257D%252520-%252520%252540LifeMadeSweeter.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span style="color: #ff0000;">
           <strong>
            PLEASE NOTE
           </strong>
          </span>
          that I have included
          <span style="color: #ff0000;">
           <strong>
            TWO
           </strong>
          </span>
          recipe boxes  one for when you have fresh precooked noodles or dry pasta noodles that you cook first on the stove-top.
         </p>
         <p>
          The second option is for thosethat have drypasta/eggnoodles and want to cook it in the slow cooker as well. It is
          <strong>
           <em>
            EASIER
           </em>
          </strong>
          on the stove but there are some people that
          <strong>
           <span style="color: #ff0000;">
            DO NOT
           </span>
          </strong>
          want to wash another pot and prefer to cook
          <em>
           <strong>
            EVERYTHING
           </strong>
          </em>
          entirely in the slow cooker so this second option is for them.
         </p>
         <p>
          <br/>
         </p>

          <div class="ERSSummary" itemprop="description">
           This versatile Asian noodle dish is flavorful and saucy with baby bok choy, carrots and chicken breasts. This makes an easy meal that can be made all in the slow cooker if desired and the vegetables and protein are easily interchangeable to suit your tastes.
          </div>
          <div class="divERSHeadItems">
           <div class="ERSServes">
            Yields:
            <span itemprop="recipeYield">
             4-6 servings
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSIngredients">
           <div class="ERSIngredientsHeader ERSHeading">
            Ingredients
           </div>
           <ul>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 pieces of uncooked chicken breast (1 lb)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 400 grams/14 ounces package of fresh Lo Mein noodles or 4 ounces of dry egg or pasta noodles of your choice (lo mein, chow mein, spaghetti, vermicelli, etc.)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 cups or 1 bunch of baby bok choy, washed and sliced
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 medium carrot, peeled and chopped or shredded into matchsticks
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 cloves garlic, minced
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon fresh ginger, minced
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             salt and pepper to taste
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <strong>
              Chicken Marinade
             </strong>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 teaspoons of low sodium soy sauce or tamari
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon of sesame oil
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon of potato or corn starch
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon of chili garlic paste *optional
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <strong>
              Sauce
             </strong>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup low sodium chicken broth
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1.5 - 2 Tablespoons oyster flavored sauce or vegetarian flavored oyster sauce
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 Tablespoon low sodium light soy sauce or Tamari
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 teaspoons of honey or sugar
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon of dark soy sauce
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon of sesame oil
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              Tablespoon of Mirin or Chinese Cooking Wine (Shaoxing wine)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             * *1-2 teaspoons of chili garlic paste (sambal oelek), red pepper chili flakes or Sriracha sauce - optional for a spicy kick
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <strong>
              Slurry for the Sauce
             </strong>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 - 3 tablespoons of potato or cornstarch (depending on how thick you want the sauce)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup of cool water
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-h50r0Rf2F4I/Um1J_Nv128I/AAAAAAAAMH4/DP72NdBtce8/s0/IMG_8677.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog4#5939484833942461378" rel="post-4228">
              <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
               <img alt="IMG_8677.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-h50r0Rf2F4I/Um1J_Nv128I/AAAAAAAAMH4/DP72NdBtce8/w450-o/IMG_8677.jpg"/>
               <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh3.ggpht.com/-h50r0Rf2F4I/Um1J_Nv128I/AAAAAAAAMH4/DP72NdBtce8/w450-o/IMG_8677.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
               </span>
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
           </ul>
           <div class="ERSClear">
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSInstructions">
           <div class="ERSInstructionsHeader ERSHeading">
            Instructions
           </div>
           <ol>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             In a small bowl, combine the chicken with the chicken marinade and leave in the fridge for at least 30 minutes.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Spray inside of slow cooker with non-stick coating spray. Add marinated chicken breasts to the slow cooker and cook on low for 1-2 hours or high for 1 hour flipping halfway through until cooked through.
             <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh5.ggpht.com/-7LdwDnSOvMI/Uo1aCCT3ICI/AAAAAAAAMH4/rweRE6HG5J0/s0/IMG_9568.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog4#5948509673852706850" rel="post-4228">
              <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
               <img alt="IMG_9568.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/-7LdwDnSOvMI/Uo1aCCT3ICI/AAAAAAAAMH4/rweRE6HG5J0/w400-o/IMG_9568.jpg"/>
               <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh5.ggpht.com/-7LdwDnSOvMI/Uo1aCCT3ICI/AAAAAAAAMH4/rweRE6HG5J0/w400-o/IMG_9568.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
               </span>
              </span>
             </a>
             <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh4.ggpht.com/-pcED0idZG4w/Uo1aoqo0lxI/AAAAAAAAMH4/PSHZovoGo-s/s0/IMG_9682.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog4#5948510337513068306" rel="post-4228">
              <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
               <img alt="IMG_9682.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh4.ggpht.com/-pcED0idZG4w/Uo1aoqo0lxI/AAAAAAAAMH4/PSHZovoGo-s/w450-o/IMG_9682.jpg"/>
               <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh4.ggpht.com/-pcED0idZG4w/Uo1aoqo0lxI/AAAAAAAAMH4/PSHZovoGo-s/w450-o/IMG_9682.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
               </span>
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Take cooked chicken out of the slow cooker on a plate. Place garlic, ginger and baby bok choy or vegetables of your choice in the bottom of your slow cooker and put cooked chicken back on top of vegetables.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Combine sauce ingredients in a bowl and pour over all the ingredients in slow cooker.
             <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh6.ggpht.com/-TT43FsilmsM/Uo1alVy7yYI/AAAAAAAAMH4/nHIAqPELE4Q/s0/IMG_9692.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog4#5948510280378730882" rel="post-4228">
              <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
               <img alt="IMG_9692.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh6.ggpht.com/-TT43FsilmsM/Uo1alVy7yYI/AAAAAAAAMH4/nHIAqPELE4Q/w450-o/IMG_9692.jpg"/>
               <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh6.ggpht.com/-TT43FsilmsM/Uo1alVy7yYI/AAAAAAAAMH4/nHIAqPELE4Q/w450-o/IMG_9692.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
               </span>
              </span>
             </a>
             <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-DkxlQ_iJWzI/Uo1am7zKvnI/AAAAAAAAMP0/eFTgzuzvbbs/s0/IMG_9697.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog4#5948510307760127602" rel="post-4228">
              <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
               <img alt="IMG_9697.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-DkxlQ_iJWzI/Uo1am7zKvnI/AAAAAAAAMP0/eFTgzuzvbbs/w450-o/IMG_9697.jpg"/>
               <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh3.ggpht.com/-DkxlQ_iJWzI/Uo1am7zKvnI/AAAAAAAAMP0/eFTgzuzvbbs/w450-o/IMG_9697.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
               </span>
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Cook on high for 30 minutes - 1 hour or low for 1.5 - 2 hours, stirring occasionally to distribute the sauce evenly.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Meanwhile, if using dry pasta or egg noodles, cook desired amount on stove according to package instructions, drain.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Add the carrots and cooked or fresh noodles into the slow cooker and use tongs to cover noodles with the sauce. Mix together the corn starch slurry in a small bowl and stir with the sauce in the slow cooker. Turn slow cooker on high and allow the sauce to thicken up - about 10 - 15 minutes.
             <a class="photoswipe" href="http://lh5.ggpht.com/-rllNZqWV2rs/Uo1apcHy71I/AAAAAAAAMPc/i5WNuNUtxXs/s0/IMG_9701.jpg" link="https://picasaweb.google.com/104357654632449509020/Blog4#5948510350796320594" rel="post-4228">
              <span class="pibfi_pinterest pibfi_float_center">
               <img alt="IMG_9701.jpg" class="aligncenter pe2-photo" src="http://lh5.ggpht.com/-rllNZqWV2rs/Uo1apcHy71I/AAAAAAAAMPc/i5WNuNUtxXs/w450-o/IMG_9701.jpg"/>
               <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/&amp;media=http://lh5.ggpht.com/-rllNZqWV2rs/Uo1apcHy71I/AAAAAAAAMPc/i5WNuNUtxXs/w450-o/IMG_9701.jpg&amp;description=Easy Slow cooker / Crockpot Chicken Lo Mein Noodles')">
               </span>
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Remove and serve hot with your favorite garnishes and sides.
            </li>
           </ol>
           <div class="ERSClear">
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSNotesDiv">
           <div class="ERSNotesHeader">
            Notes
           </div>
           <div class="ERSNotes">
            *Please note that each different slow cooker has various cooking times . These are the cooking times that worked using my Rival Crock-Pot. Please use my cooking times only as a guide or consult your manufacturer's instructions.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            *Pan frying the chicken on the stove first will enhance the flavors and texture of the chicken but is not necessary.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            * Feel free to add in any other vegetables of your choice. Broccoli, snow peas and bell peppers would work well in this dish.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            *Adding the fresh pre-cooked or cooked dry noodles JUST 20 minutes PRIOR to serving will ensure that the noodles will NOT get too soft and mushy.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            **Use pork instead of chicken or extra firm or deep fried tofu for a meatless meal. I also have a vegetarian version on my site.
           </div>
           <div class="ERSClear">
           </div>
          </div>

           3.3.3070

         <div class="easyrecipeWrapper mceNonEditable">
         </div>
         <div class="easyrecipe" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe">
          <div class="ERSName" itemprop="name">
           Slow cooker Chicken Lo Mein Noodles with Dried Pasta Cooked Directly in the Slow Cooker
          </div>
          <div class="ERSClear">
          </div>
          <div class="ERSTopRight">
           <img itemprop="image" src="http://lifemadesweeter.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/Slow-Cooker-Chicken-Lo-Mein-Crockpot-by-@LifeMadeSweeter-200x300.jpg" width="205"/>
           <div class="ERSSavePrint">
            <span class="ERSSaveBtnSpan">
             <a class="ERSSaveBtn bigoven" href="">
              Save
             </a>
            </span>
            <span class="ERSPrintBtnSpan">
             <a class="ERSPrintBtn" href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/easyrecipe-print/4228-1/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
              Print
             </a>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSTimes">
           <div class="ERSTime">
            <div class="ERSTimeHeading">
             Prep time
            </div>
            <div class="ERSTimeItem">
             <time datetime="PT15M" itemprop="prepTime">
              15 mins
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="ERSTime ERSTimeRight">
            <div class="ERSTimeHeading">
             Cook time
            </div>
            <div class="ERSTimeItem">
             <time datetime="PT4H" itemprop="cookTime">
              4 hours
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="ERSTime ERSTimeRight">
            <div class="ERSTimeHeading">
            </div>
            <div class="ERSTimeItem">
             <time datetime="PT4H15M" itemprop="totalTime">
              4 hours 15 mins
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="ERSClearLeft">
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="divERSHeadItems">
           <div class="ERSServes">
            Yields:
            <span itemprop="recipeYield">
             4-6 servings
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSIngredients">
           <div class="ERSIngredientsHeader ERSHeading">
            Ingredients
           </div>
           <ul>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 pieces of uncooked chicken breast (1 lb)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             4 ounces of dry egg or pasta noodles of your choice (spaghetti, vermicelli, gluten-free etc.)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 cups or 1 bunch of baby bok choy, washed and sliced
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 medium carrot, peeled and chopped or shredded into matchsticks
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 cloves garlic, minced
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon fresh ginger, minced
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             salt and pepper to taste
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <strong>
              Chicken Marinade
             </strong>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 teaspoons of low sodium soy sauce or tamari
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon of sesame oil
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon of potato or corn starch
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon of chili garlic paste *optional
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <strong>
              Sauce
             </strong>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup low sodium chicken broth
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1.5 - 2 Tablespoons oyster flavored sauce or vegetarian flavored oyster sauce
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 Tablespoon low sodium light soy sauce or Tamari
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 teaspoons of honey or sugar
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon of dark soy sauce
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon of sesame oil
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              Tablespoon of Mirin or Chinese Cooking Wine (Shaoxing wine)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             * *1-2 teaspoons of chili garlic paste (sambal oelek), red pepper chili flakes or Sriracha sauce - optional for a spicy kick
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             <strong>
              Slurry for the Sauce
             </strong>
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 - 3 tablespoons of potato or cornstarch (depending on how thick you want the sauce)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup of cool water
            </li>
           </ul>
           <div class="ERSClear">
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSInstructions">
           <div class="ERSInstructionsHeader ERSHeading">
            Instructions
           </div>
           <ol>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             In a small bowl, combine the chicken with the chicken marinade and leave in the fridge for at least 30 minutes.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Spray inside of slow cooker with non-stick coating spray. Add marinated chicken breasts to the slow cooker and cook on low for 1-2 hours or high for 1 hour flipping halfway through until cooked through.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Take cooked chicken out of the slow cooker on a plate. Place garlic, ginger and baby bok choy or vegetables of your choice in the bottom of your slow cooker and put cooked chicken back on top of vegetables. Combine sauce ingredients in a bowl and pour over all the ingredients in slow cooker.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Cook on high for 30 minutes - 1 hour or low for 1.5 - 2 hours, stirring occasionally to distribute the sauce evenly.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Using a slotted spoon, remove the chicken and all the vegetables out of the slow cooker.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Add dried pasta noodles into the slow cooker and use tongs to cover noodles with the sauce.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Cook on high for 20 minutes until noodles are softened and cooked through, rotating noodles every so often using tongs. Add the carrots to the crock pot.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Add the chicken and vegetables back to the slow cooker using tongs to combine well..
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Mix together the corn starch slurry in a small bowl and stir with the sauce in the slow cooker. Allow the sauce to thicken up - about 10 - 15 minutes.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Remove and serve hot with your favorite garnishes and sides.
            </li>
           </ol>
           <div class="ERSClear">
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ERSNotesDiv">
           <div class="ERSNotesHeader">
            Notes
           </div>
           <div class="ERSNotes">
            *Please note that each different slow cooker has various cooking times . These are the cooking times that worked using my Rival Crock-Pot. Please use my cooking times only as a guide or consult your manufacturer's instructions.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            *Pan frying the chicken on the stove first will enhance the flavors and texture of the chicken but is not necessary.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            * Feel free to add in any other vegetables of your choice. Broccoli, snow peas and bell peppers would work well in this dish.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            **Use pork instead of chicken or extra firm or deep fried tofu for a meatless meal. I also have a vegetarian version on m
           </div>

              You can add either precooked or uncooked chicken breast.  I used raw but the precooked chicken breast can be added at step #3 in the recipe along with the vegetables and garlic and ginger or you can also brown it on the stove top at step #7. Hope this helps and thanks for stopping by.

            <div class="comment-header">
             <div class="comment-author ">
              <img alt="" class="avatar avatar-80 photo" height="80" src="http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/5b26958ba385e89e25fb205159da7554?s=80&amp;d=identicon&amp;r=pg" srcset="http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/5b26958ba385e89e25fb205159da7554?s=160&amp;d=identicon&amp;r=pg 2x" width="80"/>
              <cite class="fn">

              </span>
             </div>
             <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
              <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/#comment-7753">
               January 8, 2014 at 6:56 am
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="comment-content">
             <p>
              Hi Naomi,
              <br/>
              If you are browning the chicken on the stove top you do not need to precook it as you will cook it through in step #7. The browned chicken gets added to the slow cooker around 30 minutes prior to serving. I added the browned chicken to the slow cooker before adding the noodles to the crock-pot to absorb the rest of the flavors from the sauce. You can also add the browned chicken to the slow cooker at the very end once your noodles and sauce are ready and then mix everything together if you want the chicken to remain crisp.  Hope that helps and please let me know if you have any other questions.
              <br/>
              Thanks for stopping by.
             </p>
            </div>

            <div class="comment-content">
             <p>
              Hi Tara, I buy mine at a local large supermarket in the asian refrigerated section near the fresh pasta.  I would imagine they sell these at any local asian grocery stores too. If you cant find the fresh ones, you can definitely use dried spaghetti noodles and cook them according to the package first before mixing them into the crockpot at the end when everything else is done. Good luck and hope that helps

            I was really excited to try making this dish after finding it on Pinterest, since I love lo mein. But for some reason, it just didnt turn out tasting right for me. Something just seemed off about the taste, and it just wasnt as flavorful as I thought it would be. I followed the directions to a T  except that I couldnt find oyster sauce so I used hoisin instead, and the store didnt have lo mein noodles either, so I bought the only kind of Asian noodles they did have, which were rice noodles. I imagine the rice noodles were where I went wrong. I see above you suggested using spaghetti instead  I never thought of that. Maybe I will have to do that next time or travel another twenty minutes to a grocery store that has more selection, to see if they have the lo mein noodles.

           <li class="comment byuser comment-author-superbooos bypostauthor even depth-2" id="comment-222401">
            <div class="comment-header">
             <div class="comment-author ">
              <img alt="" class="avatar avatar-80 photo" height="80" src="http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/5b26958ba385e89e25fb205159da7554?s=80&amp;d=identicon&amp;r=pg" srcset="http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/5b26958ba385e89e25fb205159da7554?s=160&amp;d=identicon&amp;r=pg 2x" width="80"/>
              <cite class="fn">
               <a class="url" href="http://lifemadesweeter.com" rel="external nofollow">
                Kelly
               </a>
              </cite>
              <span class="says">
               says:
              </span>
             </div>
             <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
              <a href="http://lifemadesweeter.com/2013/12/easy-slow-cooke-chicken-lo-mein-noodles/#comment-222401">
               June 15, 2015 at 2:14 pm
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="comment-content">
             <p>
              Hi Shannon,
              <br/>
              Thanks for your message, Im sorry to hear that the taste wasnt right for you but the main reason was the two substitutes that you made.
             </p>
             <p>
              The oyster sauce and the noodles are the TWO most IMPORTANT KEY ingredients for lo mein. Hoisin sauce cant be subbed for oyster sauce in this recipe.  Hoisin sauce is sweet while oyster sauce is more savory so that would alter the taste of this dish immensely. If you cant find oyster sauce, you can add in more soy sauce to make up for the lack of flavor but it will still not taste as flavorful as with oyster sauce.  Are you in the US or Canada? If so, Amazon US and Canada sell oyster sauce  although it is a bit more expensive then in stores.
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0001DMTPU/ref=pd_lpo_sbs_dp_ss_3?pf_rd_p=1944687682&amp;pf_rd_s=lpo-top-stripe-1&amp;pf_rd_t=201&amp;pf_rd_i=B00023T3J4&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_r=0WSG2NRZ4BH60JZS9GFP" rel="nofollow">
               http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0001DMTPU/ref=pd_lpo_sbs_dp_ss_3?pf_rd_p=1944687682&amp;pf_rd_s=lpo-top-stripe-1&amp;pf_rd_t=201&amp;pf_rd_i=B00023T3J4&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_r=0WSG2NRZ4BH60JZS9GFP
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="http://www.amazon.ca/Lee-Kum-Kee-Panda-Oyster/dp/B000REM4WG/ref=sr_1_2/183-5563155-5173048?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1434391808&amp;sr=8-2&amp;keywords=oyster+sauce" rel="nofollow">
               http://www.amazon.ca/Lee-Kum-Kee-Panda-Oyster/dp/B000REM4WG/ref=sr_1_2/183-5563155-5173048?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1434391808&amp;sr=8-2&amp;keywords=oyster+sauce
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              Also, rice noodles DO not cook well in the slow cooker and they should not be used for lo mein noodles. Definitely use the spaghetti noodles if you cant find lo mein noodles as they taste the closest to lo mein noodles and can be easily found anywhere.
             </p>
             <p>
              Hope this helps and please let me know if you do make this again with the ingredients I suggested. Thanks for trying the recipe out.
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="reply">

  <script>
   jQuery(document).ready(function(){
	// ready event, get a list of unique rel values for the photoswiped images
	var rels = [];
	var rel = '';
	jQuery('a.photoswipe').each(function(){
		// for each photoswipe rel, if the rel value doesn't exist yet,
		// add it to our array
		rel = jQuery(this).attr('rel');
		if(rel != undefined){
			if(!pe2_in_array(rels, rel)){
				// add this rel to our array
				rels.push(jQuery(this).attr('rel'));
			}
		}
	});

	// check to see if our rels array has been built and has any values
	if(rels.length &gt; 0){
		// we have at least one individual set of unique rels, setup photoswipe
		// for each
		jQuery.each(rels, function(key, value){
			// get this rel and create the collection
			pe2_setup_photoswipe(jQuery('a.photoswipe[rel=' + value + ']'));
		});
	}else{
		// we didn't get any rels, so attempt without rel checking
		pe2_setup_photoswipe(jQuery('a.photoswipe'));
	}
});
function pe2_setup_photoswipe(collection){
	// check to make sure our collection has records
	if(collection.length == 0){
		// nothing to do
		return;
	}

	// otherwise, setup photoswipe
	var collection_counter = 0;
	var myPhotoSwipe = collection.photoSwipe({
		// enable settings of photoswipe
		enableMouseWheel: true,
		enableKeyboard: true,
		captionAndToolbarAutoHideDelay: 0,
		imageScaleMethod: 'fitNoUpscale',
		// set the caption from the A tag's title attribute
		getImageCaption: function(item){
			// increment our image counter
			collection_counter++;

			// create the caption
			var caption = document.createElement('span');
			caption.appendChild(document.createTextNode(jQuery(item).attr('title')));

			// append a br
			caption.appendChild(document.createElement('br'));

			// define our second row separator
			var second_row_separator = false;

			// create the second row container
			var second_row = document.createElement('span');
			second_row.setAttribute('style', 'color: #BBB;');

			// create the "Image X of X"
			var num = document.createElement('span');
			num.appendChild(document.createTextNode('Image ' + collection_counter + ' of ' + collection.length));
			num.setAttribute('style', 'margin-right: 10px; margin-left: 10px;');
			second_row.appendChild(num);
			second_row_separator = true;
			// check to see if we need to output the separator
			if(second_row_separator){
				second_row.appendChild(document.createTextNode('-'));
			}

			// create the link to Google+
			var link = document.createElement('a');
			link.setAttribute('href', jQuery(item).attr('link'));
			link.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
			link.setAttribute('style', 'font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; color: #BBB; margin-right: 10px; margin-left: 10px;');
			link.setAttribute('onmouseover', 'this.style.color = \'#FF6666\';');
			link.setAttribute('onmouseout', 'this.style.color = \'#BBB\';');
			link.appendChild(document.createTextNode('View on Google+'));
			
			// append links to the second row
			second_row.appendChild(link);
			second_row_separator = true;
			// check to see if we need to output the separator
			if(second_row_separator){
				second_row.appendChild(document.createTextNode('-'));
			}

			// create the link to download
			// https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-3qAvtWntPCg/UPS4VhKFDbI/AAAAAAAAF80/Fu-YgcWCdGo/s0-d/DSC_1276.JPG
			var download= document.createElement('a');
			download.setAttribute('href', jQuery(item).attr('href').replace(/\/[^\/]+\/([^\/]+)$/, '/s0-d/$1'));
			download.setAttribute('style', 'font-style: italic; font-weight: normal; color: #BBB; margin-right: 10px; margin-left: 10px;');
			download.setAttribute('onmouseover', 'this.style.color = \'#FF6666\';');
			download.setAttribute('onmouseout', 'this.style.color = \'#BBB\';');
			download.appendChild(document.createTextNode('Download'));

			// append the download link ot the second row
			second_row.appendChild(download);
			// append the second row to the caption
			caption.appendChild(second_row);
			// return the generated caption
			return caption;
		}// end function to create the caption
	});
}// end function pe2_setup_photoswipe(..)
function pe2_in_array(array, value){
	for(var i = 0; i &lt; array.length; i++){
		if(array[i] === value){
			return true;
		}
	}
	return false;
}
